Exemption of Export Duties on Native Cloth

To be Submitted to the General Taxation and Customs Administrations for Approval

The exemption of export duties on native cloth, following requests from the Native Cloth Trade Association, the Yarn and Cloth Trade Association, and others to the General Taxation Administration, has already received verbal approval from Director Xie. These associations have also noted that the heavy tariffs levied on machine-made yarn and cloth are still reimbursed from the general taxation revenue, while native cloth, being a hand-woven product, is fundamentally exempt from general taxation, and thus the customs duty should also be completely exempt. Therefore, to achieve this goal, they yesterday contacted the General Taxation Administration on the one hand and planned to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance on the other. However, according to yesterday's contact, General Taxation Director Xie has already contacted Customs Director Zhang Fuyun, who has also agreed to the exemption. It is also heard that the two directors will jointly submit a request to the Ministry of Finance for approval.

Kailuan Failure to Resolve Order Disputes

Request Submitted to the Social Bureau for Mediation

Kailuan Mining Not Shut Down

The Coal Trade Association, regarding the dispute over Kailuan Sales Office's failure to fulfill orders, was convened for mediation by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the 16th. However, the Kailuan Sales Office and four other firms, including Yuantai, were absent, resulting in no resolution. The Trade Association found it particularly difficult to cope with the demands of its members who were awaiting orders. In addition to purchasing other types of high-priced coal within the possible range to meet the needs of customers, they have urged the Social Bureau to schedule a meeting between both parties as soon as possible to resolve the dispute.

The Kailuan Sales Office, according to the Tianjin Kailuan Mining Bureau, has stated that recent Shanghai newspapers carried Tianjin news reports stating that the bureau would suspend work in all its mining areas for four months starting April 20th, which is clearly a misrepresentation. All mining areas are currently operating as usual and have not suspended work.

Taxpayers' Association Writes to Municipal Council

Chinese Should Be Included in the Land Committee

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association wrote to the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement yesterday, stating: "Regarding your esteemed letter of April 14th in response to the unconditional collection of land taxes in the Yangshupu area, in addition to forwarding it to lawyers Ye and Yang, the Association should make the following statements: (1) Your Council did not pay attention to the meaning of 'if as stated in your letter' in the Association's letter of March 16th, which is regrettable because of the statement 'Your Council based your statement on one-sided reports, saying that the Bureau discriminates against the Chinese, which is regrettable.' (2) In the aforementioned letter, the Association mentioned the inclusion of two or three Chinese members in the Land Committee, originally hoping to eliminate the appearance of discrimination against the Chinese and to seek thorough measures to avoid discrimination against the Chinese, so as to avoid various misunderstandings that may lead to the perception of discrimination against the Chinese. However, the response did not mention this point at all, which failed to alleviate the concerns about the so-called non-discrimination against the Chinese. Accordingly, we hereby inform you, hoping that you will promptly consider the inclusion of Chinese in the local committee, so that this Association can be satisfied that there is no discrimination against the Chinese."

Hat Industry Workers Resumed Work Yesterday

The strike by workers from over ninety hat factories in the city, including Wancheng Hat Factory, has lasted for a long time. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs summoned the directors of the union the night before last, explained everything, and issued a notice to protect the resumption of work. As a result, all workers returned to the factory yesterday. The details of the situation are recorded below.

Authorities' Guidance: Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, summoned union directors Zhu Wenbiao and Zhao Xiangting to the Bureau on the evening of the 21st to question them because hat workers accused the employers of violating contracts and deducting wages, and went on strike. The employer representatives in charge had already admitted to fulfilling the contract, but the workers refused to return to work and even gathered to assault people, which was inappropriate. He also provided guidance and explanations on everything and ordered them to take responsibility and immediately persuade the workers to resume work. A notice has been issued to all workers to return to work and restore operations.

Notice of Resumption of Work: The Hat Industry Union issued a notice yesterday morning, stating: "Regarding the matter of notification, we have received the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs approval order No. 9252, which states, 'Your petition has been noted. It has been found that the employers in the industry have already admitted to fulfilling the contract regarding the wage issue, and they have also taken the initiative to publish a statement in the newspaper as requested, so there is no dispute to speak of. How can you repeatedly cause trouble on various pretexts? You must immediately instruct all workers to resume work by a set date and not delay or incur consequences.' Upon receiving this, we must notify everyone to be aware. All workers must comply and resume work by a set date, and do not delay or incur consequences. This is of utmost importance. This is hereby notified."

Protection of Work: The Shanghai Municipal Public Security and Social Bureau jointly issued a notice No. 9248 yesterday morning, stating: "Regarding the matter of joint issuance, the strike by hat workers in this case has been ongoing for many days. This Bureau of Social Affairs has previously issued a notice jointly with the Municipal Party Headquarters, limiting them to resume work within three days. If they dare to delay, it will be considered a voluntary dismissal. The deadline is approaching, and a joint notice is urgently issued. All workers in the industry must comply, resume work within the deadline, and not hesitate or be mistaken. Furthermore, the union official Wang Yuxiang, etc., because they led unemployed workers to go to various factories late at night and forcibly coerced workers who had already resumed work to strike, even assaulting and injuring people, have been investigated and dealt with by this Public Security Bureau. The workers are hereby instructed to resume work with peace of mind and not to worry. This is strictly notified."

Customs Brokerage Industry Unlikely to Resume Work

Customs Brokerage Union Persists in Old Rules

Requests Social Bureau to Implement and Promulgate Instructions

Customs brokerage workers in this city previously drafted a table of prices and short-distance agreements with three parties. However, after the Customs Brokerage Union and the Trade Association convened meetings for approval, all members opposed the establishment of a fee schedule and short-distance agreements, advocating that the fee for cotton cloth from this factory should be handled in accordance with the authorities' announcement, and the distance for the delivery of goods from the East and West Oceans should be handled according to the old rules. Therefore, the resumption of work is still unlikely for the time being. The Customs Brokerage Association has submitted a request to the Social Bureau for further mediation. The details of the situation are recorded below.

Union General Assembly: The Customs Brokerage Union held a general membership meeting at its headquarters in Panjia Lane yesterday morning at 9 a.m. to discuss the strike of cotton cloth and East-West Ocean goods. Over two hundred people attended including He Yumin, Sun Liansheng, Li Houfu, Su Houxin, Liang Jikang, Zhou Juxing, Ren Xinxiang, etc. Su Houxin was elected chairman, and Ren Xinxiang served as the recorder. The chairman reported on the cause of the strike, which was caused by the cotton cloth industry, causing repeated delays. Yesterday, the Social Bureau convened a mediation, and the three parties held consultations in the Zhaoshang Yu, and immediately resolved as follows: (1) Regarding the case of cotton cloth fees from this factory, all members advocated that in accordance with Social Bureau Announcement No. 9097, cotton cloth merchants who buy cloth from Haojia (trading houses) should pay an additional fee of 34 copper coins per piece in addition to the general tax payable, which should be transferred from the cotton cloth Hao merchants to the workers; (2) The distance for the delivery of East and West Ocean goods was from the east to Huishan Wharf, from the south to Dada Wharf, and from the west to Lihe Warehouses near Erbai Du Bridge before May 30th. After May 30th, it was from the east to Mitsubishi Wharf, from the south to Dada Wharf, and from the west to Lihe Warehouses. Moreover, this strike was entirely due to the issue of cotton cloth fees from this factory, which has nothing to do with the distance of East and West Ocean goods. The cotton cloth industry's proposed new distance table is obviously blackmail. It was resolved on the spot that the distance of East and West Ocean goods must be handled in accordance with the old rules.

Association General Assembly: The Customs Brokerage Trade Association held a general membership meeting at its association in Qingyunli, Shandong Road at 2 p.m. yesterday, attended by forty-two firms, including Wu Zhaohua of Tiantaiheng and Shi Zhibin of Yuanfeng Kunji. Chairman Shi Zhibin first reported on the recent situation of the strike of cotton cloth and East-West Ocean goods from this factory, as well as the mediation convened by the Social Bureau and the consultations that the three parties had conducted on their own. Then, discussions began: (1) Zhu Xieshen, representative of Xinyuanchang, proposed that although the newly opened Six Wharves followed the method before May 30th, the situation is different now than it was in the past. In the past, barges could be used, but now cars must be used. The amount stipulated in the newspaper cannot be recognized. I suggest that we still follow the method of dealing with Zhang. All members unanimously expressed their approval. (2) The chairman proposed that whether there are prices or open restrictions for open wharves should be discussed further. All members did not agree and could not sign any conditions with the Cotton Cloth Association. (3) Please discuss the issue of collecting wharf donations again. All members advocated that the old rules should still be followed and that the industry should not collect them. (4) It was decided that the only way is to list the various methods and present them to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs for fair processing: (A) Cotton cloth from this factory and East-West Ocean goods cannot be combined into one place. Opening the wharf is a matter of foreign goods and has nothing to do with this dispute. (B) The collection of cartage by the Cotton Cloth Industry Association has been a custom for decades, how can it be overthrown suddenly? (C) Wharf donations, inspection fees, and stamp duty are outside the issue of cartage and have nothing to do with this strike fee, so they should not be mixed up. (D) The letters from the various customers indicate that the Hao merchants have expressed their desire to follow the past rules, so there should be no problem with the Cotton Cloth Association collecting the various fees, which can be used as an excuse. (E) In addition to the association's attempt to persuade the union to resume transportation, the Social Bureau should be requested to implement instructions, ordering the Cotton Cloth Association to follow the old rules and not change them. The resolution was passed. (5) Pan Mengkang, representative of Dachuantong, proposed that if cotton cloth brokers are willing to pay for cartage, customs brokerage workers should be asked to transport them as before. It was resolved that this should be done after the union representatives and all the workers have consulted.

Jin Xin Labor Dispute to be Arbitrated Today

The Jin Xin Silk Weaving Factory has been on strike for more than thirty days. The Municipal Government has scheduled arbitration for 2 p.m. today. Dayouyu Oil Factory Idling Dispute

Mediated by the Social Bureau

The Dayouyu Oil Factory at No. 36 Suzhou River Road in Western Shanghai had a dispute with its workers idling on the job this month. The factory, unable to bear the losses, requested assistance from the competent authorities. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs scheduled mediation for the case the other day. Ling Wei Wu and Lin Xuezhi, representatives of the capital side, and Qiu Zhulian and Sun Kouming, representatives of the labor union, attended. Zhu Guilin was the chairman, and Wang Zhizhen was the recorder. After a long discussion, four items of settlement were signed: (1) If the factory lacks raw materials, it may adjust shifts as necessary. (2) If the number of 15 vehicles is reduced to 10, the 15 workers will be distributed among the shifts to work on average. When it is reduced to five vehicles, the next hand will be temporarily suspended from work. (3) The above measures will last until the end of the autumn inventory. (4) In the future, workers' work should be based on the normal production volume as a standard, and should not be intentionally reduced.

The Shanghai Accountants Association held a spring general membership meeting at the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association yesterday. The standing committee members of the presidium were Xi Yushu, Wang Haifan, and Jiang Wanping. The meeting opened as usual. Chairman Xi Yushu delivered the opening remarks, Standing Committee Member Jiang Wanping reported on the progress of the association's affairs, Accounting Committee Member Wang Haifan presented various accounting documents and reported on the income and expenditure situation. Supervisory Committee Member Xu Yongzu reported on the supervision of the association's affairs and finances, and Supervisory Committee Member Sun Zhongyao reported that he considered the Executive Committee's implementation of the association's affairs and financial management to be appropriate. The chairman reported that some members were in arrears with their membership fees, some for six months and some for one year. Should they be handled according to the regulations, or should they be notified again? It was resolved that: (1) Article 36 of the association's rules would be amended and passed, the amendment being "The members meeting must have a quorum of one-quarter of all members to be held" (2) The provisions of Article 39 regarding representation rights would be amended to limit one member to one right of representation, which was passed. Subsequently, because some of the members present left, there was no quorum, and the meeting was adjourned.

Recent Tragic Reports from Shaanxi Disaster

More and more wheat seedlings are withering and dying

Mr. Zhu will come with funds for relief

The Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for the Shaanxi Disaster has successively received disaster reports and requests for relief from various counties in Shaanxi, like snowflakes, one after another. The general situation is that spring seedlings are suffering from drought, relief grain is cut off, more people are dying, and more people are fleeing. Yesterday, the association received a telegram from Mr. Cui Junhao (19) of the Xi'an North China Charity Federation (the relief agency established by Zhu Ziqiao), stating that Lou Yuqiao will return to the province on a certain date. The telegram from Xiaoxian was received, stating that 20,000 yuan in relief funds have been collected. The remaining 20,000 yuan will be handed over by Mr. Zhang to Mr. Rao to distribute in Qian County. Relief work in Mei County has been completed, with 11,500 yuan distributed, only one yuan per family. The disaster situation in that area is even worse than the famine relief efforts of last year. The scene is heartbreaking. Of the original 118,000 people, only 63,000 remain. Of those who can survive without relief, there are only 15,000 to 16,000 people. The rest cannot survive without relief. There has been no rain for a long time, and the drought continues. Temporary relief requires 47,000 to 48,000 yuan, so that each person can receive one yuan. The three counties of Qi, Fu, and Xing are under investigation, and tickets are being distributed in advance. Please allocate funds quickly for immediate distribution. According to the recent report from the Whole House Relief Association, over 30,000 people have fled elsewhere, about 50,000 have died, and more than 16,000 women have been sold. The original paddy fields are still viable, but the residents of the upper areas are naked and starving. Recently, there have been consecutive light rains. Attached is a submission from Cui Xianlou. Another telegram (20th) was received from the Shaanxi Provincial Relief Association, stating that after investigating the disaster victims in Fengxiang, a total of 96,714 people have committed suicide by jumping into wells, falling off cliffs, or taking poison, as well as those who have starved to death. More than 10,000 people have fled or been sold cheaply. Since the beginning of spring, there have been only two rain showers, which barely wet the ground. Wheat seedlings are withering, and grain prices are rising daily. Furthermore, it is the season between harvests, and more than 200,000 dying lives may not escape starvation. Please provide relief quickly to save the lives of the people, etc. The association is posting advertisements to continue raising funds, and is also urging Mr. Zhu Ziqiao by telegram to go to Shaanxi to plan for distribution as soon as possible. A telegram has been received from Mr. Zhu from Dalian, stating that he will take the Changchun Maru to Shanghai to collect relief funds and personally take them to Shaanxi. It is said that the Changchun Maru is scheduled to arrive on the 26th of this month.

Page 15

Local News

Ye Zhongfang Rushes Back from Beiping

Faces Chen Xueli in Court

Ye Zhongfang's Profound Affection

Chen Xueli Lacks Conscience

A Most Embarrassing Flying Kiss

Swallowing Pills, Preparing a Suicide Note

│Judge Hopes for Reconciliation Between the Two Parties│

Chen Xueli, whose original name was Chen Xiuzhen, and who previously worked as a dancer at the Chang'e Dance Hall in the French Concession, is the daughter of the late lawyer Chen Zhigang, and is now nineteen years old. When she worked as a dancer, she met Ye Zhongfang, the grandson of Ye Chengzhong. They were as close as mandarin ducks and butterflies, and their love was extraordinary. Later, with the consent of both parties and with lawyer Jiang Baoli as a witness, they signed a document and rented a house to live together. However, a month ago, due to a breakdown in their relationship, Ye left Shanghai for Beiping, and Chen returned to her mother's home. Initially, Ye's mother and wife sued Chen in court, but at Ye's urging, the lawsuit was withdrawn. Later, Chen's mother, Chen Yan, hired Xue Jiaqi and Wang Zuxun to sue Ye in the Special District Local Court for enticing and abandoning [her daughter]. The Special District Court had already held a preliminary hearing on the afternoon of the 8th of this month, but because the defendant was in Beiping and did not attend, the hearing was adjourned. The details have already been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the adjourned hearing was held again. The court convened at 2:00 PM, still presided over by Judge Xiao. The plaintiff and defendant both appeared in court to confront each other. As a result, they were ordered to go outside for reconciliation, and the hearing was adjourned again. The details of the hearing are recorded separately below.

Plaintiff and Defendant Arrive in Court on Time　This case was originally scheduled for continuation today, but the court, to avoid overcrowding, changed it to yesterday. Therefore, only about a hundred people were in attendance. The plaintiff, Chen Yan, accompanied by her daughter Xiuzhen, arrived at the Third Criminal Court of the Special Court at around 2:00 PM and sat in the witness seat to await instructions. Xiuzhen was wearing a gray coat with white floral trim and a fur collar, flesh-colored stockings, and dark blue satin flat shoes. Ye Zhongfang also rushed back to Shanghai from Beiping a few days ago to prepare for the confrontation. He arrived at the court at around 2:00 PM and sat in the reporter's seat, wearing a suit and appearing relaxed. At 2:30 PM, Judge Xiao Xiefen appeared in court for the hearing. Ye's lawyers, Jiang Yiping and Dong Yu, also appeared in court on time to defend him.

Why Not Sue Sooner After Knowing About the Enticement? 　Judge Xiao first asked Ye Zhongfang his age, origin, and address. Ye replied that he was from Zhenhai, Zhejiang, 23 years old, and lived at 601 Jiaozhou Road. He was currently studying. Then, Chen Yan was called to the stand and asked why she was suing Ye Zhongfang. She replied that he had enticed her daughter Xiuzhen to run away. She was asked how old her daughter was. She replied that she was 19 years old this year. She was asked if her daughter was betrothed to anyone. She replied no. She was asked when she was enticed away. She replied that it was when she was 17 years old, that is, December 22nd of the year before last. She was asked where. She replied that at that time, she had returned to her hometown for her husband's funeral on the 22nd, and she had agreed with her daughter to return together. The defendant took the opportunity to come and coax her daughter to go out for refreshments, and she never returned home. She was asked when she returned. She replied that it was around May of last year. She was asked if she had searched for her. She replied that she had searched and had reported it to the French police. She was asked if she had placed an advertisement in the newspaper. She replied no. She was asked if she had asked her daughter where she had been after she returned. She replied that her daughter said she was at Ye Zhongfang's place. She was asked how they got together. She replied that she only knew that Ye had taken her away and didn't know what had happened. She was asked if her daughter had gone out again after she returned. She replied yes. She was asked since her daughter returned in May of last year and she knew that she had been enticed away by Ye Zhongfang, why she had only come to sue now. She replied that she hadn't sued before because she had many children and lacked the strength. Now, because Ye's mother and wife were suing her in court, she was also suing him. She was asked if she would not have sued if Ye Zhongfang hadn't sued her. She replied that if she had the strength, she would have sued anyway. She was asked if her daughter was Ye Zhongfang's concubine. She replied that she didn't know.

Leaving His Wife to Marry Me 　Judge Xiao then called Chen Xiuzhen to the stand and asked her how old she was. She replied that she was 19 years old, from Shanghai, and lived at 19 Qingshun Lane, Rue Ste. Marie. She was asked what her occupation was. She replied that she had no occupation now. She was asked who Chen Yan was. She replied that she was her birth mother. She was asked if it was true that she was enticed away by Ye on December 22nd of the year before last, as her mother had said. She replied that it was. She was asked how she was enticed away. She replied that he asked her to go for refreshments. After the refreshments, he took her to the train station. However, he first took her to the Xin Xin Hotel to open a room, and then rented a house at 45 Mingde Lane. She was asked if her mother knew. She replied no. She was asked if he had taken her for refreshments. She replied yes. At that time, he didn't allow her to go home, saying that he wanted to marry her. She was asked if she was willing. She replied that he said he would divorce his wife, so she was willing. But her mother didn't know. She was asked if she had lived with his wife after going to Ye's house. She replied yes. She was asked if she was his concubine. She replied that she didn't know at first, but later she found out when she saw that he had children, but it was too late to do anything.

It's Okay to Be a Concubine If Life is Good 　She was asked if they had signed a contract. She replied that they had signed it at lawyer Jiang Baoli's office. She was called there by Ye, and she had brought a copy with her (which was presented to the court by her lawyer, Xue Jiaqi). She was asked if her mother knew. She replied no. She was asked when she told her mother. She replied that it was about May or June, when she went to visit her mother because she was ill, that she told her mother. She was asked when she went back after running away on December 22nd. She replied that she went back after about five or six months. She was asked if she had told her mother about this after she went back. She replied that she had told her. She was asked what her mother had said at the time. She replied that her mother said it would be okay as long as life was good.

Being a Concubine Doesn't Necessarily Mean Money 　She was asked if she had received any money. She replied no. She was asked why she hadn't received any money. The contract stated that she was a concubine and that if she was abandoned in the future, she would receive 20,000 yuan. She replied that being a concubine didn't necessarily mean money. She was asked if she could be independent if she was someone's concubine. She replied that she didn't tell her mother because she had been with him for five or six months before she came back.

Chen's Mother Allowed Her to Live with Her Daughter　Judge Xiao then turned to Ye Zhongfang and asked if he had any response to what the Chen women had said. Ye replied that he certainly had his own defense, saying that according to the other party, he went to Chen's house and took Xiuzhen out, so why wouldn't Chen's mother have sued at that time? He met Xiuzhen at the dance hall and danced with her, and they got along very well. He had bought many things for her and her mother. One day, he was drunk, and her mother told him to sleep at her house and told her daughter to stay with him. That night, they had relations. After that, they often stayed outside. Because they were shy, her mother advised him not to spend so much money outside and to live in a house at her house. He bought a lot of furniture, wallpapered the walls, and installed electric lights. They lived at her house for about two or three months. This could all be proven. He also agreed to give her ten yuan every day. Later, because he didn't have the money to provide, her mother was unhappy, and he couldn't bear it, so he stopped going. Later, Xueli tried to commit suicide by swallowing opium because her mother was pressuring her. She was cured by Dr. Sun Kejin's injection. Later, Xiuzhen repeatedly invited him by phone to meet her at the Carlton. After he met her, he knew that she and her mother could no longer get along. She asked him to rent a house. Before renting the house, they first stayed at Room 11 of the Xin Xin Hotel. At this time, she asked lawyer Zhang Ding to write a letter and publish a statement that she was breaking away from her mother. Later, they moved to 45 Mingde Lane. At the same time, they signed a contract. Her younger siblings came to Mingde Lane and went out to play with them. Later, due to lack of money, they moved to the old house on Jiaozhou Road. At the old house, she and her mother didn't get along, and his mother helped to mediate. What he said was all true, and there was no falsehood.

Her Conscience Isn't Bad, She Treats Me Very Well 　After Ye finished his statement, Judge Xiao asked when he started living with Xiuzhen. He replied that it was in May of the year before last, when Xiuzhen was working as a dancer at the Chang'e Dance Hall. He was asked if he took Xiuzhen out on December 22nd. He replied that she asked him to the Carlton Theater to discuss it with him because Xiuxiu Zhen wanted to leave and didn't want to go home. He was asked if her mother had returned to her hometown at that time. He replied that he didn't know. He was asked when Xiuzhen came to his house. He replied that it was after August of last year. At that time, her conscience wasn't bad and she treated him very well. And because the expenses were too high, they returned to the old house. Before that, they lived on the third floor of 45 Mingde Lane for about five or six months. He was asked if her mother knew. He replied that she certainly knew. He and Xiuzhen went out to play every day, and everyone knew. Even her younger siblings were often together. He was asked if her mother agreed to him living with Xiuzhen. He replied that if her mother didn't know when they signed the contract, she could sue. At this time, lawyer Jiang Yiping asked the court to ask Chen Yan if the defendant had lived in her house for three months, so she knew that she had agreed.

Knowing in Advance, Acknowledging Afterwards　Lawyer Jiang also said that the electric lights and wallpaper in Chen's house were all installed by the defendant, which proved that Chen Yan knew in advance and acknowledged it afterwards. Ye Zhongfang's cohabitation with Chen Xiuzhen did not break away from the person enjoying parental rights, so how could it be called enticement? Lawyer Xue Jiaqi also stated that the only thing that needed to be studied was whether Chen Yan knew about Xiuzhen's departure. There was an advertisement published by lawyer Zhang Ding on behalf of Chen Yan searching for her, which could prove it. He then presented the newspaper to the court. Judge Xiao then asked Chen Yan if the defendant had lived in her house for three months, as the defendant claimed. She replied that he had, but the defendant had come to rent the remaining rooms, and he had come with several friends, saying that he wanted to divorce his wife. She was asked if it was possible for one person to rent two houses to live in. She replied that the defendant had never come to live there. She was asked if Ye Zhongfang and Xiuzhen had a relationship at that time. She replied that she didn't know. She was asked if she had any evidence that Ye Zhongfang had enticed her daughter away. She replied that it was when Ye came and called her away, and he had taken away all the electric lights. She also didn't know that they were living together in Mingde Lane. She was asked if she had seen the newspaper her daughter published on January 24th of last year. She replied that she had seen it, and she had asked lawyer Chen Jinrong to write a letter to ask about it. She was asked why she had waited until October to write the letter when her daughter published the newspaper in January. She replied that it was because she was ill and was afraid that there would be letters before that. She was asked if she went to ask Xiuzhen to come back, and if she had come back. She replied that Ye didn't dare let her come back. She was asked if she didn't object to her daughter signing a contract with Ye to be his concubine. She replied that at first, it was said that they were getting married, but later she found out that she was a concubine.

How Could You Forget About Cohabitation?　At this time, the plaintiff's lawyer, Wang, asked Ye Zhongfang when he had rented the house in Mingde Lane. He replied that it was the year before last. He was asked what month. He replied that he had forgotten. He was asked when he had terminated the lease. He replied that he had forgotten. He was asked if he had also forgotten that he had lived with Xiuzhen. He replied that they had lived together for four or five months, and this was the most memorable thing, so how could he forget?

Chen Yan Refuses to Answer the Judge 　After lawyer Wang finished asking questions, Ye's lawyer, Dong Yu, also stood up and asked for the court's permission to question Chen Yan. He asked how many years her daughter had studied, but she refused to answer. He asked her again and again, but she not only didn't answer, but said that the judge could ask, but he couldn't ask her. Lawyer Jiang then stood up and declared that Chen Yan was refusing to answer the judge and should be noted by the court. Judge Xiao then told her that the lawyer could ask her and she should answer what she knew. Lawyer Xue also advised her to answer, so she replied that she had studied, but she had forgotten how many years. Lawyer Dong then asked if she had asked Zhu Xinying to go to Ye's house to ask for 20,000 yuan. She replied that he could go ask Ms. Zhu. She was asked if she had received fifty yuan from him. She replied that he had sent it to her. She was asked if Ye had been to her house. She replied that it was because her daughter had been beaten by Ye, so his mother had sent it to her. Lawyer Jiang then asked Chen Yan if Ye Zhongfang had rented a house at her house. She replied that he had, it was a small house that he rented.

Adjourn the Hearing and Reconcile Outside the Court　At this point, Judge Xiao then turned to Chen Xiuzhen and asked why she had filed a lawsuit when she had been with Ye Zhongfang for two years. (She replied) My mother wanted to sue him, not me. (He asked) Your mother knew about it before, so why does she still want to sue him now? (She replied) My mother has already said the reason why my mother wanted to sue him, I don't need to say it again. After Judge Xiao heard the case, he announced to the lawyers of both parties that the plaintiff and defendant had been together for two years, so why did they go to court? It would be better to go outside and try to reconcile. Lawyer Jiang Yiping then stood up and stated that he was willing to accept the court's ruling and try his best to reconcile, while the plaintiff's lawyer requested that the defendant be detained or released on bail because the defendant had not arrived last time. Judge Xiao said that the defendant was a person with property and did not need to be detained or released on bail, and ordered that the case be adjourned for two weeks to try to reconcile, and then adjourned the court.

Zhongfang Blows a Kiss, Xiuzhen is Ashamed　After the court was adjourned, Chen Xiuzhen was surrounded by photographers when she left the court with her mother. However, Chen's mother expressed her unwillingness and quickly hid beside her uncle, Mr. Yan, lowered her head and left the court, walking north. Ye Zhongfang was also waiting for Xiuzhen in front of the court. When Xiuzhen left the court, Ye shouted "Madam," but Xiuzhen didn't look back. It was a coincidence that Xiuzhen and her mother walked north to Haining Road to take a rickshaw, and then traveled east on Qipu Road, while Ye Zhongfang and Jiang Yiping happened to be getting into a car at the back door of Qipu Road when they suddenly saw the Chen women coming towards them. Ye immediately shouted "Xueli Madam" and put his hand to his mouth, making a kissing gesture. The Chen women made a gesture of shame with their fingers. Ye also shouted "Xueli, you should have some conscience!" Xueli replied, "Are you still talking about conscience with you now?"

Swallowing Pills, Preparing a Suicide Note　Before arriving in court, Ye Zhongfang had taken ten sleeping pills and prepared several suicide notes to his mother, relatives, friends, and newspaper reporters, preparing to commit suicide. He was only prevented from committing suicide after being monitored and persuaded by relatives and friends. A copy of his self-statement is recorded below. "I will go to a place where I don't want to see Xue, to avoid the humiliation of being detained. A couple who were deeply in love have come to this end today. Although it can be said that Zhong is responsible for his own misfortune, Xue is too heartless. Looking back on the past, I can't help but feel moved. Zhong abandoned his family and changed his name to join the military academy, just to seek death. But who can know why I died? Therefore, I decided to skip school and arrive in court on time, enduring the pain to express my bitter heart, so that people in society can fully understand and dispel the previous misunderstandings about this case. Zhong sacrificed everything for Xue. Everything Zhong shouldn't have done, he did for the sake of loving Xue. Disobeying my mother is the first thing, abandoning my family is the second, spending lavishly is the third, and other minor faults are hard to list. Zhong was abandoned after sacrificing everything, and today Xue hates Zhong like a worn shoe. She even colluded with her mother to criminally accuse Zhong, breaking Zhong's heart and ruining Zhong's reputation. If Xue still has a heart, she should ask herself in the quiet of night if she feels that this method is too harsh. At the hearing on the 8th, Zhong did not attend because his leave was not approved. Xue's mother's lawyer then said that Zhong was absent because he was afraid of being punished. It should be known that everything Xue's mother said in her complaint was a paper tiger that would be punctured with a little poke. After Zhong met Xue, he not only went in and out of her house day and night, but also lived with Xue in the drawing-room of her house for about three months at her command. Wallpapering and buying wooden furniture, installing electric lights, everything was done arbitrarily without her permission. And when Xue was at the Chang'e, she had a big fight with her girlfriend for dancing with Zhong, and she also came to the scene to dissuade her. The facts are all there and can be proved, and cannot be falsely accused. Before Xue lived with Zhong, she asked lawyer Zhang Ding to negotiate with her mother on her behalf, and stated that if Zhong seduced her, then lawyer Zhang should be questioned first. Later, my mother tried to reconcile with her mother at the Atlantic Restaurant because Xue had no home to go to. This can also be investigated. And Xue broke away from her family after fighting with her mother, and after living with Zhong, they also signed a contract at lawyer Jiang's office with the consent of both parties. But today, she came to court with her mother to participate in the prosecution, without saying that Zhong still loves her like the flesh of his heart. Even if Zhong is truly unfaithful and abandons her, she can file a lawsuit on her own according to the contract. But today, Xue is not doing this. Instead, she is reversing her previous approach to cooperation, working with her mother to fabricate words and put Zhong in trouble. She must have other thoughts in her heart, intending to falsely accuse him. Therefore, this case is not so much a love lawsuit as a black-hearted lawsuit. Things have come to this point, and Zhong's heart is as bitter as eating huanglian, and no one knows it. Only Xue is the love of my life. Although she has left me, my love for her has not diminished. I also hope that she can marry a satisfactory man and grow old together, and no longer have conscious love affairs. Don't fail my one and a half years of careful protection, don't fall, don't be deceived, take the path of light and enter the door of happiness. I will die with my eyes closed. Zhong also has no face to ask for the family's pity, and no face to ask friends for help to salvage this broken situation. I made my own mistakes, I suffer my own hardships, and life is worse than death."

Gold Bars Hidden Inside Turtle Shells

Smugglers Have Ingenious Ideas

Unexpectedly Discovered by Customs Officers

The "Chinese-language Newspaper" reports that yesterday (the 21st), when the Nagasaki Maru was leaving the port, customs officers found ten gold bars being smuggled out hidden inside turtle shells. When the customs officers boarded the ship for inspection, they caught sight of six baskets of turtles, which made them suspicious. They also noticed that there were several dead turtles at the bottom of the baskets, which made them even more suspicious. They took out the live ones and examined the dead ones, and found gold bars hidden inside the shells. The smugglers had hollowed out the internal organs of the four turtles and inserted the gold bars inside. At first glance, there was nothing unusual, and they thought it was a perfect plan, but they didn't expect that their inability to move would arouse the suspicion of the customs officers. Since the National Government strictly prohibited the export of gold, smugglers have emerged one after another. A few days ago, someone tried to smuggle gold bars in eel baskets, but they were also detected by customs officers and confiscated. It is also reported that customs officers seized 175 pounds of opium on another ship on Monday.

Special Court Guard

Steals Firearms from the Public Security Bureau

Secretly Discovered by Lu Ying

The Guard is Detained Awaiting Legal Action

The guards in the Special District Local Court were transferred from the Municipal Public Security Bureau when the court was established and were responsible for protection. One of the guards, named Meng Xiushan, was from Hebei Province. After each shift, he often returned to the Public Security Bureau to visit his old brothers. Recently, he took the opportunity to steal five Mauser pistols and more than 300 rounds of ammunition from the bureau, secretly took them to the Special Court, and hid them in a box in the guard's bedroom in the flat house on the left side of the Special Court's main entrance. No one knew about it at first. It was not until about 3:00 AM on the night of the 19th of this month that the bureau discovered the missing firearms. The investigation team leader, Lu Ying, secretly investigated and learned that Meng had stolen them. The next morning, Captain Lu went to the Special Court and asked the prosecutor's office to transfer the guard for investigation. Chief Prosecutor Zhou approved the request. Later, Captain Lu took Meng Xiushan back to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for strict investigation. Meng could not deny it and confessed, and also revealed where he had hidden the firearms. At 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, Captain Lu returned to the Special Court and found the guns and ammunition, all intact, in the box in the guard's bedroom. He immediately took them back to the bureau and reported them to Director Chen of the Public Security Bureau for instructions on how to handle the matter according to the law.

Remodeling of the Confucian Temple into a Park

The Second Phase of the Project Will Be Bid on Today

The first phase of the project to remodel the Confucian Temple in this city into a park was won by the San Mori Construction Company, and it is expected to be completed by the end of May. The southern wall of the Confucian Temple has been completely demolished and replaced with brick piers, spaced about five or six feet apart. Evergreen trees will be planted between the piers so that people outside the park can see the stone archways inside the park. The stone archways have been completely removed due to years of decay, and San Mori will renovate all the stone pillars and rebuild them. A large stone bridge over the lotus pond in front of the Dacheng Hall and two small stone bridges, as well as a stone bridge on the side of the Pantang Pond, must be demolished and rebuilt. Other renovations in the park are currently under construction. The second phase of the project, which is to renovate the historical sites, including the Dacheng Hall, the Hulen Hall, the Chong Sheng Ancestral Hall, and the Kuixing Pavilion, is currently being tendered and is scheduled to be bid on the 25th of this month. The construction of the library and concert hall is being handled by the Municipal Works Bureau, and the bidding will also be held today. The layout and design of the museum and hall in the future will be carried out by the Municipal Education Bureau. Today is the date for the bidding of the second phase of the project. The municipal government and the Municipal Education Bureau have sent personnel to the bureau to supervise the bidding. The procedures and preparations for the construction are summarized as follows: (1) Scope of work: The concert hall and library will use steel and reinforced concrete as the framework, and ordinary masonry materials for the walls. The doors, windows, and roof frames will all be made of wood. The lower part of the exterior walls will be plastered with cement, and the upper part will be sprayed with cement slurry. The interior walls will be brushed with white lime and colored powder, as specified by the architect. The floor will be paved with cement flower tiles. (2) Location of buildings: The location of the concert hall and library is inside the Confucian Temple on Confucian Temple Road in the west gate of Shanghai. The exact location is shown in Figure 701. (3) Surveying and leveling: The contractor shall determine the various boundary lines, levels, and draw the gray lines of the buildings, and set up corresponding marking piles. This boundary line level shall be inspected and approved by the architect before work can begin. (4) Templates: The contractor shall draw various templates. The surveyor's rod shall be approved by the architect before work can begin according to the drawings. (5) Photographs: The contractor must take one photograph of each of the above projects, at least once a month, to show the progress of the project. The parts and locations to be photographed shall be indicated by the architect. One copy of the photograph shall be submitted to the owner and sent to the architect. The negatives shall be numbered sequentially and the date shall be noted. (6) Models: Various decorations must be made into models first. The contractor shall hire a high-quality model craftsman to handle it. Work shall not begin until the model has been approved by the architect. (7) Stone sections: All stone sections, as specified in the drawings, shall use Suzhou sesame stone and shall be approved by the architect. There shall be no mixed colors or other defects to detract from the aesthetics.

Chen Mutao Sentenced

To One Year and Six Months Imprisonment

With a Fine of 1,500 Yuan

Chen Mutao, the deputy director of the savings department of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, gradually embezzled 64,000 yuan of savings funds. Recently, fearing detection during the handover of accounts, he attempted suicide by poisoning. He was sent to the hospital for treatment and then handed over to the Special District Local Court. Chen admitted to misappropriating the bank's funds, claiming it was to support his brother's expenses. The official ordered him to be held pending sentencing, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning was the date for the sentencing of the case. The police escorted Chen to the First Criminal Court of the Special Court, where Judge Xu Jiashi presided and announced the verdict. Chen Mutao was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for continuous embezzlement of property under his management during his duties, and fined 1,500 yuan. If the fine is not paid, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of three yuan per day, but not exceeding one year. French Municipal Council

Awards Long Service Medals

More Than Twenty Recipients

The French Concession Municipal Council awarded long service medals to Chinese and Western employees of the council at noon on the 14th of this month (Saturday) in the council's courtyard. The medals were presented by Mr. Cogelin, the French Consul-General in Shanghai and Chairman of the Council. This is the first time the council has awarded such medals. Recipients of these medals must have served for a long time and made significant contributions. The medals are divided into gold, silver, and bronze. The gold medal is for those who have served for more than 40 years, the silver for more than 30 years, and the bronze for more than 20 years. More than twenty people received medals this time. Only one Chinese employee, Gu Baixing, the chief accountant of the accounting department, received the gold medal, having served for 45 years. A Western employee, Mr. Raymond, received the gold medal for 41 years of service. The remaining medals were awarded to employees of the tax collection office, engineering office, and police department. The ceremony was a grand occasion. It is also reported that Mr. Hu Fangjin, the comprador of the council, whose subordinates received the most medals, hosted a banquet at his private residence, Shangganglu, on the 22nd to celebrate.

Shanghai Bank Building Completed

Office and Apartment Rental Section to Open Next Month

Recently, construction projects have flourished in Shanghai, and the construction of office and apartment buildings for rent has also increased rapidly. The new Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank building has now been completed, standing majestically on Ningbo Road. The structure of the bank's headquarters is particularly bright and magnificent. The interior of the building includes office and apartment rentals, bordering Jiangxi Road and Beijing Road, making it a leader among Chinese-owned buildings. It is said that the office space has already been fully rented, with only a few apartments remaining. The apartment system originated in Western countries. Affluent families rent apartments, enjoying the convenience of modern facilities such as elevators, hot and cold water, steam, and refrigerators, suitable for both winter and summer. This allows the owner and hostess to adapt to the seasons with ease, without the need for servants. Moreover, this facility is similar to a cooperative operation by the tenants, which is in line with the principles of consumer cooperation. The apartments in the Shanghai Bank all have these features. The apartment building is only a hundred yards from the Bund, providing ample convenience for leisure and comfort. Those who have already rented will start renting next month, along with the office space.

Passengers Must Have Air Pillows

Yesterday, this newspaper received a letter from Mr. Liu Changrong of the Anhui Sanhe Weighing Station: "Dear Sir, I recently read in your newspaper that many large ships along the Yangtze River and the coast have had accidents, causing many passenger injuries and deaths, which is distressing to hear. Here is a method to ensure safety when traveling by boat, which is the rubber cloth air pillow sold in foreign goods stores. It can be used as a pillow at ordinary times. Take it with you when traveling by boat. In case of danger, you can hold the pillow in your arms, and even if you fall into the water, you will not drown. The method is to first weave a mesh cover with a thicker cotton rope or thread, put the pillow into the mesh, and tie the four corners with larger rope loops, which will be strong and durable. Grasp firmly with both hands in case of danger to ensure safety. I am not an advertising representative for the pillow industry. I am writing this out of concern for the pain of death in domestic travel, and I implore the chief editor to publish it in your newspaper to protect people's lives."

Resolution of the Eighth Annual Shareholders' Meeting

The Truth About the Zhongzhou Hotel Suicide

The Deceased Was a Chauffeur

Committed Suicide Due to Excessive Debt

A man and a woman came to the Zhongzhou Hotel in Maijiaquan the other day and stayed in room 107. They committed suicide by poisoning. When they were discovered, the man was beyond救药 and died, and the woman was still barely breathing and was sent to the hospital for treatment, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the deceased was Zhang Jingtao, also known as Zhang Er. The woman was Zhang's mistress. Zhang was a chauffeur for Mr. Xie, an official at the Jianghai Customs. Although his monthly income was not low, his expenses were very high, and he was already in financial straits. Three months ago, he returned to his hometown in Yangzhou to marry a woman named Dong, which cost a lot of money. Most of the money was borrowed from Indians, totaling no less than a thousand yuan. After marrying Dong, he brought her to Shanghai, intending to live with his mistress to save household expenses, but Dong strongly opposed it, so his austerity policy could not be implemented. Recently, the debts he had incurred were gradually coming due, and he was unable to repay them, so he was sued by the creditors. Ten days ago, Zhang planned to abandon his career as a driver and take Dong away from Shanghai, but she stopped him. So, he left home alone last Thursday and never returned. Dong did not know where he had gone and searched everywhere. Unexpectedly, he had gone to a hotel with his mistress and committed suicide by drinking poison. Dong has an older brother who is a police officer in the General Police Station, number 2459. When he heard about the suicide, he went to the mortuary on Feilun Road to identify the body. He saw that it was his sister, so he rushed to notify her sister at 376 Hengbang Bridge, North Sichuan Road, to prepare clothes and a coffin. Yesterday morning, after Guo, the prosecutor of the Special District Local Court, came to the mortuary to examine the body clearly, Dong and her brother filed a case and requested to claim the body for burial.

Old Man Dies a Heroic Death

Rushing Out to Put Out a Fire, He Fell and Suffocated

In front of the China Public School in Wusong, a Chen surname food stall suddenly caught fire on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Zheng Youzhang, a neighbor from Henan, rushed out to put out the fire in a heroic act. Unexpectedly, he walked too fast, and being nearly sixty years old, he fell and suffocated to death. After the incident, the local police station ordered the head of the 39th district to report to the local court yesterday morning for an inquest. The deceased's wife, Zheng Lu, submitted a request to the court to waive the inquest.

Man Dies from Untreated Broken Leg

At about 11 o'clock yesterday morning, a wounded man, about 30 years old, was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by a young man in a rickshaw. After entering the hospital, the young man helped the injured man into the examination room to wait for treatment. The young man pretended to go out to pay the rickshaw fare, but did not return for a long time. The people in the hospital were very surprised and reported to the police station, who ordered Chinese and Western detectives to come and search, but they could not find him. The injured man had broken his tibias in both legs. When he arrived at the hospital, he was already unconscious and bleeding from his mouth and nose. Resuscitation was ineffective, and he died at around 1:00 p.m. He was wearing a blue-gray cloth padded jacket, a blue cloth short shirt, and black cloth padded pants, looking like a worker.

Abducted Car Found

The private car, number 2436, of Jin Runxiang, the manager of the Minfeng Paper Company, was abducted the day before yesterday by bandits who also took his younger brother Anxiang, and they disappeared. After the incident, the Public Security Bureau and the police station sent out detectives to search for their whereabouts. Because the car had fled from Jiangwan Road, You, the chief of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau, ordered Police Officer Niu Kaiping to lead the police to search along Jiangwan Road. Until about 11:30 a.m. yesterday, car number 2436 was found near the Dijia Hamu Road in Dong Ti Yu Hui Road. Police Officer Niu ordered the police to drive the car back, waiting for the owner to claim it.

Record of the Li Church Supervisory Committee

The Supervisory Committee of the Shanghai Li Church Federation convened a meeting of all leaders yesterday, with 49 people attending. Su Yongchun was elected as the chairman. First, He Songting, a supervisor, reported on the purpose of the meeting. The following issues were discussed: (1) The motion that all public offices requesting to appoint leaders must be examined and qualified by the federation before requesting the executive committee to issue certificates was resolved and passed. (2) The letter from the Lao Dexiu Tang public office requesting Cheng Zhixiang as the director was resolved. After checking the federation's list of leaders, it was found that there was no such person, and a letter of denial was sent back. (3) The motion drafted by Committee Member Jiang on the rules of procedure for the leaders' meeting was resolved, amended, and passed. (4) The motion to hire Hua Anyu as a clerk for the federation was resolved and passed. (5) The motion to nominate a committee to review new leaders for each public office was resolved. Wu ZhanKuei, Wang Rurong, Liu Bingyu, and Zhong Sanhe were publicly nominated. Finally, Committee Chairman Zhang Yichen gave a speech on the true meaning of the Li Church, and the meeting adjourned.

Dasin Silk and Satin Store Business is Booming

The Dasin Silk and Satin Store at the intersection of Shilu and Sanma Road is known as the only large-scale, modern silk and satin store in Shanghai that is trusted by the public for its genuine goods at fair prices. The store will hold a 21-day spring sale starting on the 22nd of this month. Yesterday was the first day of the sale. From morning to night, customers were extremely crowded. It is estimated that hundreds of bolts of various new silk and satin products were sold throughout the day. In addition, film star Hu Die and others specially introduced the store's new outfits and personally ordered dozens of spring outfits from the store's new outfit department. The tailoring of these new outfits is said to be a style that has never been seen before in Shanghai. The booming business is truly the leader in the Shanghai silk industry.

Silk and Satin Industry and Refining Industry Have Hopes of Reconciliation

The silk and satin industry and the refining industry had a dispute over settlement of accounts, which could not be resolved. The refining industry, feeling that the losses were too great to continue operating, had announced that it would close down all operations from the 20th to show its determination. It is now heard that the silk and satin industry, in order to maintain the relationship, has sent a letter to the refining industry, asking them to continue trading and suggesting that both parties send representatives to hold a joint meeting, and invite the competent authorities to attend the meeting to jointly find a proper solution. It is hoped that after this meeting, all the difficulties between the two industries can be resolved.

Fire in Huangjia Road in the City

At 12:20 p.m. yesterday, a fire broke out on the upper floor of the house of Wang Meiqing, number 123 Dong Huangjia Road inside the Xiaonanmen in the city. The fire quickly broke through the roof and spread to four rooms on the upper floor of number 121 Ma Yongxing bell shop, number 125 Zhi Renli overpass building, and number 127 Dai Yaolai weaving shop. The fire was quickly extinguished by the fire brigade. Fortunately, the lower floors were preserved. The cause of the fire was that Wang's wife was ill and bedridden, and she ordered her child to decoct medicine in the room carelessly, causing the fire. Afterwards, the police from the Third Section of the First District summoned and fined the arsonist.

The Five Mountains Swordsmen is a Bestseller

The Five Mountains Swordsmen is published by the Central Bookstore and distributed by the World Bookstore on Four Horse Road. Since its release, it has been enthusiastically welcomed by readers. It has now been published in its third edition. It will be sold out in a few days.

Tao Society Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition Last Three Days

The Tao Society Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition has been exceptionally popular with visitors and buyers. A large number of ancient and modern paintings and calligraphy works have been sent by specially invited painters and calligraphers. All of them are famous works. In order to allow art lovers to appreciate them, the exhibition will be extended for three days (until April 25th). The location is still in Xizhongheli, opposite the China Bookstore on Four Horse Road. It will be closed after the deadline.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday: The weather will change from cloudy to overcast. There will be rain and heavy fog on the Fujian coast. The coastal winds from Shandong to the south will be from the north to the northeast. The wind in the Bohai Sea will turn to the south. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 66.9 degrees and the lowest was 49.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 66.7 degrees and the lowest was 56.1 degrees.

Letters to the Editor

Dear Chief Editor,

I have read in your newspaper's local news column that a guest shop owner was accused of bigamy and abandonment. The protagonist, Sun Runyu, was mistakenly identified by your newspaper as the owner of Yuxing Pawnshop. The colleagues in our pawnshop were very surprised to read this. Our pawnshop was founded solely by Sun Runshen, without any external shareholders. The Sun Runyu mentioned in your newspaper has nothing to do with our pawnshop. The involvement of the owner of Yuxing Pawnshop is probably due to inaccurate rumors. We are deeply afraid that the outside world will confuse right and wrong and spread rumors, so we have written to you to request a correction. Sincerely, The Colleagues of Yuxing Pawnshop.

Dear Sir,

When the Dalun Real Estate case was heard in court yesterday, the arguments made by our lawyer on behalf of the tenants regarding jurisdiction were slightly different from those reported in today's newspaper. Here is a summary for your kind correction. Sincerely, Lawyer Wang Youling.

The Supreme Court believes that the case involves a dispute over the lease, not just a dispute over eviction, so Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Civil Procedure Law cannot be applied as primary jurisdiction, but Article 11 of the same law should be used to determine jurisdiction. Both the Civil Procedure Law and the Civil Procedure Regulations have provisions for agreed jurisdiction. Therefore, a case that is originally a primary jurisdiction case can be subject to local jurisdiction by agreement of the parties, and a case that is originally a local jurisdiction case can be subject to primary jurisdiction by agreement of the parties. In the first instance of this case, Dalun Company clearly argued according to the primary jurisdiction case, and the court clearly accepted the case according to the primary jurisdiction case, and the tenants did not raise any objection to the lack of jurisdiction before the debate. According to Article 40 of the Civil Procedure Law and Article 40, Paragraph 2 of the Civil Procedure Regulations, it has become an agreed primary jurisdiction case without any doubt. The Supreme Court ignored this situation and believed that the case should be accepted by the same court for the third instance, which is a factual error, not an error in legal opinion. After the establishment of the High Branch Court, the court submitted a request to the Judicial Yuan for an interpretation of where the third instance of the primary jurisdiction case accepted by the former High Court of Appeal should be accepted. The Judicial Yuan's Directive No. 160 instructed that the primary jurisdiction cases of the former Temporary Court should be the High Branch Court as the court of third instance (i.e., the court of final instance) has become a precedent. The appeal in this case was filed after the establishment of the High Branch Court. According to the provisions of the Civil Procedure Law and the Civil Procedure Regulations on agreed jurisdiction, the Judicial Yuan's Directive No. 160 is not to be accepted by the Supreme Court. Now that it is a judgment of the third instance, it is what the Civil Procedure Law calls the judgment court not following the legal system. An appeal for retrial can be filed against a judgment court that does not follow the legal system. However, this case has been remanded for retrial, which is different from a completely final case. It is doubtful whether a retrial can be filed because the jurisdictional part has already been determined. However, a retrial can only be filed after it is completely determined, then all procedures will be carried out in vain, which will cause many obstacles in fact. How should it be remedied? The Judicial Yuan should be asked for instructions. It should be solemnly declared that the jurisdictional issue raised by this lawyer is based on the provisions of the Civil Procedure Law and the Civil Procedure Regulations on agreed jurisdiction, and the Judicial Yuan's Directive No. 160 that the primary cases of the former Temporary Court should be accepted by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court for the third instance. Therefore, it has nothing to do with the Supreme Court's interpretation of Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Civil Procedure Law and Article 11 of the same law. Therefore, it has no conflict with the Supreme Court's opinion.

Dear Sir,

I have just read a news item in your newspaper's local news column entitled "Lu Lixia's Regret for a Misstep." The excerpt from the indictment stated, "Lu Lixia intended to apply for a position as a female employee at the Shanghai Guohuo Bank. Unexpectedly, the defendant, Lan Wenlin, a colleague at the bank, took a liking to her at first sight and repeatedly tried to seduce her." Our bank has never recruited female employees, and there is no such person as Lu Lixia or Lan Wenlin among our employees. Please correct this on our behalf. Sincerely, Shanghai Guohuo Bank, April 22.

To the Editor-in-Chief of the Shanghai Shenbao,

I have read a report in your newspaper of the 19th (reporting date) entitled "Resolution of the Dispute between Old and New Workers on the Gonghe Wheel." This is not in accordance with the facts. (1) The Seamen's Union did not send representatives. (2) The old workers and the comprador both expressed their objections to the Wuhan Municipal Government's intention to retain the new workers. (3) The old workers only signed in at the arbitration meeting for the case and did not sign off on any solutions. Please investigate and correct this. Sincerely, The Organizing Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Industrial Joint Federation, Ma Yin.

Art World

Oil Painting and New Green

— Written by Yamamoto Kanae, Translated by Chen Baoyi

For me, using oil painting to sketch landscapes, the color green is the most difficult to express. When it comes to… fields and hills, they all become a heavy, solid green. River beaches and such shine like lead roofs. Tree trunks, appearing with a grape-like color in the height of summer, are not easy to start with. Although I am deeply moved by that kind of weighty, masculine "nature," once I try to depict it, the result is just an ordinary depiction. …This is because there is no embellishment in the summer scenery. …Although plants contain an ample quantity (Volume) and present a magnificent beauty, the changes in color and shade cannot compare to spring and autumn. This is consistent with winter, so I would rather draw "sketches" in summer and winter.

When it comes to new green, I feel that oil painting is the best way to express it. …Isn't that kind of bright, intense color just like the colors freshly squeezed from a paint tube: Cadmium Citron, Cadmium Cair, Vert Emeraude, and so on? …For example, the tender leaves of the persimmon tree are a color with a little "Cadmium Citron" mixed into "Vert Emeraude." …The new green of the Kaname tree (tree name) is a color with a little Carance "red" mixed into "Cadmium Cair." The new sprouts of the oak tree are a color with Indian Yellow added to "Cadmium Citron" to make it slightly dim and obscure, and then a touch of "blue." …The new green of the larch is a bit like scallions. It is better to use blue than green; it is still a color blended with "Cadmium Citron" and those colors. Generally speaking, these can all be used directly from the colors on the "palette" without error… Green—and new green—is as bright as a flower. …During the season of new green, the soil also appears with a loveliness that one cannot help but feel. …It seems as soft as butter, as loose as cake, and as heavy as beef, and it is moist even in the daytime. …This color is really a color that can tempt the desire for oil painting. …The soil is good, of course, but the sky at that time is also beautiful. Mostly, it is cloudy with a tinge of water color, making the new green of the oak and camphor trees appear as bright as frost. That sky is also something that belongs to oil painting.

However, oil paintings depicting new green are rarely seen in recent exhibitions. In the past, there were probably various paintings of new green, but there doesn't seem to be any work that has become a well-regarded one. …I remember clearly that the year before last, in the Western masterpieces exhibited by the Asahi Shimbun, there was a large work by Monet depicting the new green of hazel trees. …It still used his elastic brushstrokes to thickly pile up bright paints to express the fresh midday sunlight. …This painting can be considered one of the representative works in Monet's production. —Generally speaking, in the paintings of the early Impressionists, "green paintings" are quite common. Sisley, for example, also painted many new greens of poplars and sycamores. …Pissarro excelled at green orchards. …And Renoir's olive groves and Cezanne's pine trees… Thinking of them one by one, there seem to be quite a few. Sisley, when expressing the bright green color of the shade, has a habit of embellishing it with grape color, which, I feel, makes the painting vulgar and inelegant. …On the deep green of the olive trees painted by Renoir, there is a mixture of Emeraude, Carance, Bleu (blue), and so on, making it as smooth as deep nephrite. —Cezanne seems to not use Emerald; any bright color seems to be made with "yellow" and "blue." Moreover, in the shaded parts, there is almost no trace of "red." …He probably uses his soft brush, dipped in a thick amount of paint. …The brush is not picky, does not slide, but is quiet and never diminishes. …He certainly dwells on the symphony of colors of the Motive (the subject of the painting, i.e., the scene being depicted—translator's note) in his eyes and depicts it. …That painting of green trees is truly beautiful.

When it comes to Japanese works, in my past memory, there are the watercolor paintings of Miyake Kokki. When Mr. Miyake first returned from abroad, he frequently painted many green paintings. I remember that before I was an art student, everyone at that time was fascinated by Mr. Miyake's "green paintings." Ishii Hakutei's watercolor painting, titled "Tender Persimmon Tree," was also well-received. …Yamashita Shintaro also publishes his beautiful green forests every year. …As for recently, in the previous Shun'yokai exhibition, Umehara Ryuzaburo exhibited a work with a large group of green trees and shadows as the foreground "Lake Haruna," which made me recall the clear charm of the green mountains.
